--  DDL for Trigger TRG_ANSWER
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "TRG_ANSWER" 
 AFTER 
 INSERT ON ADMIN_ANSWER
 FOR EACH ROW
 BEGIN
 UPDATE ADMIN_QNA A
    SET A.ADMIN_ANSWER_YN = 'Y'
  WHERE A.ADMIN_QNA_NO = :NEW.ADMIN_QNA_NO;
  END;
/
ALTER TRIGGER "TRG_ANSWER" ENABLE;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Trigger TRG_COUPON
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "TRG_COUPON" 
  AFTER 
 INSERT ON COUPON_USE_HISTORY
 FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
 UPDATE COUPON C
    SET C.COUPON_USE_YN = 'Y'
  WHERE C.COUPON_NO = :NEW.COUPON_NO;
END;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "TRG_COUPON" ENABLE;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Trigger TRG_POINT
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "TRG_POINT" 
  AFTER 
 INSERT ON POINT_HISTORY
 FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
 IF :NEW.GETUSE_TYPE_GU = 'G'
   THEN
     UPDATE POINT P
        SET P.POINT = P.POINT + :NEW.POINT
      WHERE P.POINT_NO = :NEW.POINT_NO;  
 END IF;
 IF :NEW.GETUSE_TYPE_GU = 'U'
   THEN
     UPDATE POINT P
        SET P.POINT = P.POINT - :NEW.POINT
      WHERE P.POINT_NO = :NEW.POINT_NO;
 END IF;
END;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "TRG_POINT" ENABLE;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Trigger TRG_REPORT_HISTORY
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "TRG_REPORT_HISTORY" 
  AFTER 
 INSERT ON REPORT_HISTORY
 FOR EACH ROW
 BEGIN
 UPDATE REPORT R
    SET R.REPORT_STATUS = 'Y'
  WHERE R.REPORT_NO = :NEW.REPORT_NO;
END;
/
ALTER TRIGGER "TRG_REPORT_HISTORY" ENABLE;
